window.ezAnalyticsStatic = true;

function analyticsAddScript(script) {
	var ezDynamic = document.createElement('script');
	ezDynamic.type = 'text/javascript';
	ezDynamic.innerHTML = script;
	document.head.appendChild(ezDynamic);
}
function getCookiesWithPrefix() {
    var allCookies = document.cookie.split(';');
    var cookiesWithPrefix = {};

    for (var i = 0; i < allCookies.length; i++) {
        var cookie = allCookies[i].trim();

        for (var j = 0; j < arguments.length; j++) {
            var prefix = arguments[j];
            if (cookie.indexOf(prefix) === 0) {
                var cookieParts = cookie.split('=');
                var cookieName = cookieParts[0];
                var cookieValue = cookieParts.slice(1).join('=');
                cookiesWithPrefix[cookieName] = decodeURIComponent(cookieValue);
                break; // Once matched, no need to check other prefixes
            }
        }
    }

    return cookiesWithPrefix;
}

    <script>
function readCookie(name) {
    var nameEQ = encodeURIComponent(name) + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) === ' ')
            c = c.substring(1, c.length);
        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0)
            return decodeURIComponent(c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length));
    }
    return null;
}
let cookie_prefix = 'fox_1_'
let user_darkmode = readCookie( cookie_prefix + 'user_darkmode' );
if ( 'dark' == user_darkmode ) {
    document.body.classList.add('darkmode');
} else if ( 'light' == user_darkmode ) {
    document.body.classList.remove('darkmode');
}
</script>

        <h1 class="post-title single56__title component56">Monkeypox warning in Spain: Country registers highest number of cases in Europe</h1>
    <div class="meta56 component56">
        <div class="meta56__item meta56__author">
        by <a href="https://www.theolivepress.es/spain-news/author/alextheolivepress-es/" itemprop="url" rel="author"><img data-del="avatar" src="https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/ALEX-FACEBOOK-PIC-150x150.jpg" class="avatar pp-user-avatar avatar-80 photo " height="80" width="80">Alex Trelinski</a>    </div>    </div>
        </div>
                    <div class="single56__thumbnail single56__block">    <figure class="single_thumbnail56 thumbnail56--standard post-thumbnail">
        <img width="720" height="500" src="https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe.jpeg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="Mpox latest in Spain: Health chiefs call emergency meeting as number of cases per region is revealed" loading="eager" decoding="async" fetchpriority="high" srcset="https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe.jpeg 720w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe-300x208.jpeg 300w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe-490x340.jpeg 490w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe-60x42.jpeg 60w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe-24x17.jpeg 24w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe-36x25.jpeg 36w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-warning-in-Spain-Country-registers-highest-number-of-cases-in-Europe-48x33.jpeg 48w" sizes="(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px">            </figure>
    </div>
            </div>
        <div class="container container--main single56__outer">
            <div class="primary56">
                    <div class="single56__body single56__block">
        <div class="entry-content single56__content single56__post_content single56__body_area">
        
<p><strong>SPAIN has recorded the highest number of monkeypox cases in Europe since the start of the current outbreak in April 2022.</strong></p>



<p>A total of 8,101 cases have been reported- almost double that of the second-placed country, France.</p>



<p>This year has seen 260 confirmed cases with nearly half in the Madrid area and 90% of those affected were unvaccinated.</p>



<p><strong>READ MORE:</strong></p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><a href="https://www.theolivepress.es/spain-news/2024/02/26/monkeypox-virus-is-detected-in-two-adults-and-a-six-year-old-child-in-spains-andalucia/"><em>Monkeypox virus is detected in two adults and a six-year-old child in Spain’s Andalucia</em></a></li>



<li><a href="https://www.theolivepress.es/spain-news/2023/01/30/man-in-spains-valencia-facing-jail-term-fine-for-text-blaming-lgbtq-community-as-origin-of-monkeypox/"><em>Man in Spain’s Valencia facing jail term, fine for text blaming LGBTQ+ community as origin of monkeypox&nbsp;</em></a></li>
</ul>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="490" height="368" src="https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-490x368.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-349707" srcset="https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-490x368.jpg 490w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-300x225.jpg 300w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-60x45.jpg 60w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-24x18.jpg 24w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-36x27.jpg 36w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1-48x36.jpg 48w, https://www.theolivepress.es/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/Monkeypox-1.jpg 1300w" sizes="(max-width: 490px) 100vw, 490px"></figure></div>


<p>16 infections have been reported between July 5 and August 5 by the Carlos III Institute.</p><div class="addrop-wrap" data-id="322261"><script async="" src="https://securepubads.g.doubleclick.net/tag/js/gpt.js"></script>

<p>Practically all of the cases(98%) are in males, aged between 6 and 68 years, although six out of ten were between 30 and 49 years old, bringing the average age to 37.</p>



<p>Three out of four presented general symptoms, such as fever (the most frequent), asthenia, sore throats, muscle pain or headache,</p>



<p>Rashes that developed were located in the anogenital area in 76.1% of cases.</p>



<p>Of the 213 out of 260 infections this year, 16.4% of people reported having had close contact with a probable or confirmed case.</p>



<p>The most likely form of transmission was sexual intercourse in 80% of monkeypox infections with the overwhelming number of cases involving gay or bi-sexual men.</p>

<p>To contact the newsdesk out of regular office hours please call +34 665 798 618 We are available over the Christmas and Easter holidays</p>
<p>Voted Spain‘s number one expat newspaper and ‘second in the world’, by 27,000 people polled by UK marketing group Tesca. Also dubbed “The best English newspaper in Spain,” according to the UK’s Rough Guide. The Olive Press is the English language newspaper for Spain. Local news, in particular, from the Costa del Sol, Andalucia, Alicante, Murcia and Mallorca, plus national news from around Spain. A campaigning, community newspaper, the Olive Press launched in 2006 and represents the huge and growing expatriate community in Spain – with over 100,000 printed copies monthly, 50,000 visitors a day online we have an estimated readership of more than 500,000 people a month.</p>
